cyclopean_walls_poly = {
	start = 1000
	date = 1.1.1
	time = { months = 240 }
	build_cost = 500
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 1
	type = monument
	
	build_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					area = polyrrenia_area
					area = gortyn_area
					area = knossos_area
					area = hierapytna_area
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	on_built = {
		FROM = { add_prestige = 25 }
	}
	
	on_destroyed = {}
	
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					area = polyrrenia_area
					area = gortyn_area
					area = knossos_area
					area = hierapytna_area
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			capital_scope = {
				OR = {
					area = polyrrenia_area
					area = gortyn_area
					area = knossos_area
					area = hierapytna_area
				}
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}
	
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}
		region_modifier = {}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
	
	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		
		province_modifiers = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.2
		}

		area_modifier = {
			
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
		
		country_modifiers = {
			garrison_size = 0.1
		}
	}
	
	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		
		province_modifiers = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.3
		}

		area_modifier = {
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
		
		country_modifiers = {
			garrison_size = 0.15
		}
	}
	
	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}
		
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}
		
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		area_modifier = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.4
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
		
		country_modifiers = {
			garrison_size = 0.2
		}
	}
}

prosphorion_harbor = {
	start = 1086
	date = 1.1.1
	time = { months = 240 }
	build_cost = 500
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 2
	type = monument
	
	build_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				tag = PPP
				tag = BYS
				capital_scope = {
					region = propontis_region
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	on_built = {
		FROM = { add_prestige = 25 }
	}
	
	on_destroyed = { }
	
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		AND = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					tag = PPP
					tag = BYS
					capital_scope = { region = propontis_region }
				}
			}
			OR = {
				culture_group = hellenic_group
				culture_group = italic_group
				culture_group = bosporan_group
			}
		}
	}
	
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		AND = {
			FROM = {
				OR = {
					tag = PPP
					tag = BYS
					capital_scope = { region = propontis_region }
				}
			}
			OR = {
				culture_group = hellenic_group
				culture_group = italic_group
				culture_group = bosporan_group
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}
	
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
	
	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		
		province_modifiers = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.3
		}

		area_modifier = {
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
		
		country_modifiers = {
			naval_forcelimit_modifier = 0.1
			global_tax_income = 6
		}
	}
	
	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2500
		}
		
		province_modifiers = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.6
		}

		area_modifier = {

		}

dur_untash = {
	start = 3470
	date = 1.1.1
	time = { months = 240 }
	build_cost = 500
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 1
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = elamite_religion
			religion = mesopotamian_religion
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = elamite_religion
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		FROM = { add_splendor = 50 }
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = elamite_religion
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			religion = elamite_religion
			religion = mesopotamian_religion
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = elamite_religion
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
				has_harmonized_with = elamite_religion
				has_harmonized_with = mesopotamian_religion
				AND = {
					has_reform = syncretism_reform
					ROOT = { tolerance_to_this = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			religion = elamite_religion
			religion = mesopotamian_religion
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = elamite_religion
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
				has_harmonized_with = elamite_religion
				has_harmonized_with = mesopotamian_religion
				AND = {
					has_reform = syncretism_reform
					ROOT = { tolerance_to_this = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			local_tax_modifier = 0.2
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_governing_cost = -0.1
			local_monthly_devastation = -0.05
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 0.25
			administrative_efficiency = 0.01
		}
		on_upgraded = {
			FROM = { add_splendor = 75 }
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			local_tax_modifier = 0.4
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_governing_cost = -0.15
			local_monthly_devastation = -0.1
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 0.5
			administrative_efficiency = 0.025
			religious_unity = 0.1
		}
		on_upgraded = {
			FROM = { add_splendor = 100 }
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 360
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 4000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			local_tax_modifier = 0.6
		}
		area_modifier = {
			local_governing_cost = -0.2
			local_monthly_devastation = -0.15
			local_tax_modifier = 0.1
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 1
			administrative_efficiency = 0.05
			religious_unity = 0.2
		}
		on_upgraded = {
			FROM = { add_splendor = 150 }
		}
	}
}

akhetaten = {
    start = 6254
	date = 1.1.1
	time = { months = 240 }
	build_cost = 2000
	can_be_moved = no
	starting_tier = 0
	type = monument
	
	build_trigger = {
	    religion = atenism
	}
	
	on_built = {
		FROM = {
			add_legitimacy = 100
			add_prestige = 40
			add_estate_loyalty = { 
       			estate = estate_priesthood 
        		loyalty = -15 
	   		}
		}
	}
	
	on_destroyed = {

	}
	
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = atenism
				has_harmonized_with = egyptian_religion
				has_adopted_cult = cult_serapis
				has_adopted_cult = cult_aten
			}
		}
    }
	
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = atenism
				has_harmonized_with = egyptian_religion
				has_adopted_cult = cult_serapis
				has_adopted_cult = cult_aten
			}
			treasury = 2000
		}
	}
	
	keep_trigger = {
	always = yes
	}
	
    tier_0 = {
	    upgrade_time = {
		months = 48
		}
	    cost_to_upgrade = {
		    factor = 2000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		
		}
		area_modifier = {
		
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
			legitimacy = 0.05
			prestige = 0.05
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		
		}
	}
	
    tier_1 = {
	    upgrade_time = {
		months = 48
		}
	    cost_to_upgrade = {
		    factor = 2000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		
		}
		area_modifier = {
		
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
			legitimacy = 0.10
			prestige = 0.10
			build_cost = -0.05
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		
		}
	}
	
	tier_2 = {
	    upgrade_time = {
		months = 48
		}
	    cost_to_upgrade = {
		    factor = 2000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		
		}
		area_modifier = {
		
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
			legitimacy = 0.25
			prestige = 0.10
			build_cost = -0.05
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		
		}
	}
	
	tier_3 = {
	    upgrade_time = {
		months = 48
		}
	    cost_to_upgrade = {
		    factor = 2000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		
		}
		area_modifier = {
		
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
		legitimacy = 0.50
		prestige_decay = -0.01
		build_cost = -0.1
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		
		}
	}
}

babylonia_temples = {
	start = 2500
	date = 1.1.1
	time = { months = 960 }
	build_cost = 1000
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 2
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = punic_religion
			religion = mesopotamian_religion
			religion = elamite_religion
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = punic_religion
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
				religion = elamite_religion
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		FROM = { add_splendor = 200 }
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
			}
			add_stability = -1
		}
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = punic_religion
			religion = mesopotamian_religion
			religion = elamite_religion
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = punic_religion
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
				religion = elamite_religion
				has_harmonized_with = punic_religion
				has_harmonized_with = mesopotamian_religion
				has_harmonized_with = elamite_religion
				AND = {
					has_reform = syncretism_reform

			religion = punic_religion
			religion = mesopotamian_religion
			religion = elamite_religion
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = punic_religion
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
				religion = elamite_religion
				has_harmonized_with = punic_religion
				has_harmonized_with = mesopotamian_religion
				has_harmonized_with = elamite_religion
				AND = {
					has_reform = syncretism_reform
					ROOT = { tolerance_to_this = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {

	time = { months = 240 }
	build_cost = 500
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 1
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			culture = persian
			culture_group = elamite_group
		}
		OR = {
		    owner = { tag = ANH }
			owner = { primary_culture = persian }
			owner = { culture_group = elamite_group }
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		FROM = { add_splendor = 50 }
	}

	on_destroyed = {
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			culture = persian
			culture_group = elamite_group
		}
		OR = {
		    owner = { tag = ANH }
			owner = { primary_culture = persian }
			owner = { culture_group = elamite_group }
		}
	}
	
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			culture = persian
			culture_group = elamite_group
		}
		OR = {
		    owner = { tag = ANH }
			owner = { primary_culture = persian }
			owner = { culture_group = elamite_group }
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {}

	tier_0 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}
		province_modifiers = {
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			local_tax_modifier = 0.25
			allowed_num_of_buildings = 1
		}
		area_modifier = {
			trade_goods_size_modifier = 0.1
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
			culture_conversion_cost = -0.15
			core_creation = -0.1
			governing_capacity = 100
		}
		on_upgraded = { FROM = { add_splendor = 100 } }
	}

	tier_2 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 2000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			local_tax_modifier = 0.45
			allowed_num_of_buildings = 1

ur_city_temple = {
	start = 2517
	date = 1.1.1
	time = { months = 240 }
	build_cost = 500
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 1
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			religion = mesopotamian_religion
			religion = elamite_religion
			religion = arab_religion
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
				religion = elamite_religion
				religion = arab_religion
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		FROM = { add_splendor = 50 }
	}

	on_destroyed = {
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			religion = mesopotamian_religion
			religion = elamite_religion
			religion = arab_religion
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
				religion = elamite_religion
				religion = arab_religion
				has_harmonized_with = mesopotamian_religion
				has_harmonized_with = elamite_religion
				has_harmonized_with = arab_religion
				secondary_religion = mesopotamian_religion
				secondary_religion = elamite_religion
				secondary_religion = arab_religion
				AND = {
					has_reform = syncretism_reform
					ROOT = { tolerance_to_this = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		is_capital = yes
		OR = {
			religion = mesopotamian_religion
			religion = elamite_religion
			religion = arab_religion
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
				religion = elamite_religion
				religion = arab_religion
				has_harmonized_with = mesopotamian_religion
				has_harmonized_with = elamite_religion
				has_harmonized_with = arab_religion
				secondary_religion = mesopotamian_religion
				secondary_religion = elamite_religion
				secondary_religion = arab_religion
				AND = {
					has_reform = syncretism_reform
					ROOT = { tolerance_to_this = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {}

	tier_0 = {

		}

		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			local_tax_modifier = 0.4
			local_production_efficiency = 0.2
			allowed_num_of_buildings = 1
		}
		area_modifier = {
		}
		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 0.25
			state_governing_cost = -0.1
			spy_offence = 0.1
		}

				AND = {
					has_reform = syncretism_reform
					ROOT = { tolerance_to_this = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		has_temple_building = yes
		OR = {
			religion = luwian_religion
			religion = cybele
		}
		OR = {
			religion = mesopotamian_religion
			religion = elamite_religion
			religion = punic_religion
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				religion = mesopotamian_religion
				religion = elamite_religion
				religion = punic_religion
				has_harmonized_with = mesopotamian_religion
				has_harmonized_with = elamite_religion
				has_harmonized_with = punic_religion
				secondary_religion = mesopotamian_religion
				secondary_religion = elamite_religion
				secondary_religion = punic_religion
				AND = {
					has_reform = syncretism_reform
					ROOT = { tolerance_to_this = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	start = 4921
	date = 1.1.1
	time = { months = 240 }
	build_cost = 500
	can_be_moved = no
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	starting_tier = 0
	type = monument

	build_trigger = {
		has_temple_building = yes
		OR = {
			religion = armenian_religion
			religion_group = persian_group
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				has_harmonized_with = armenian_religion
				has_harmonized_with = persian_group
				secondary_religion = armenian_religion
				secondary_religion = iranian_religion
				secondary_religion = zoroastrianism
				secondary_religion = zurvanism
				AND = {
					has_reform = syncretism_reform
					ROOT = { tolerance_to_this = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	on_built = {
		FROM = { add_splendor = 75 }
	}

	on_destroyed = {
	}

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		has_temple_building = yes
		OR = {
			religion = armenian_religion
			religion_group = persian_group
		}
		FROM = {

				has_harmonized_with = armenian_religion
				has_harmonized_with = persian_group
				secondary_religion = armenian_religion
				secondary_religion = iranian_religion
				secondary_religion = zoroastrianism
				secondary_religion = zurvanism
				AND = {
					has_reform = syncretism_reform
					ROOT = { tolerance_to_this = 2 }
				}

		}
	}

		has_temple_building = yes
		OR = {
			religion = armenian_religion
			religion_group = persian_group
		}

				has_harmonized_with = persian_group
				secondary_religion = armenian_religion
				secondary_religion = iranian_religion
				secondary_religion = zoroastrianism

					has_reform = syncretism_reform

			}

	}

			months = 0
		}

		region_modifier = {}
		country_modifiers = {
		}
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1000
		}
		province_modifiers = {
			local_tax_modifier = 0.15
			local_defensiveness = 0.1
		}
		area_modifier = {

		region_modifier = {}
